\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00185}00185 \textcolor{comment}{/* Flags for new pointer objects */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00186}\mbox{\hyperlink{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_a1a125b0e9c551bb9cdeb21b8e5be5b57}{00186}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SWIG\_POINTER\_OWN           0x1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00187}00187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00188}00188 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00189}00189 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00190}00190 \textcolor{comment}{   Flags/methods for returning states.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00191}00191 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00192}00192 \textcolor{comment}{   The SWIG conversion methods, as ConvertPtr, return an integer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00193}00193 \textcolor{comment}{   that tells if the conversion was successful or not. And if not,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{   an error code can be returned (see swigerrors.swg for the codes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{   Use the following macros/flags to set or process the returning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{   states.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{   In old versions of SWIG, code such as the following was usually written:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00201}00201 \textcolor{comment}{     if (SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj,vptr,ty.flags) != -\/1) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{comment}{       // success code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00203}00203 \textcolor{comment}{     \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00204}00204 \textcolor{comment}{       //fail code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00205}00205 \textcolor{comment}{     \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00206}00206 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00207}00207 \textcolor{comment}{   Now you can be more explicit:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00208}00208 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00209}00209 \textcolor{comment}{    int res = SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj,vptr,ty.flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00210}00210 \textcolor{comment}{    if (SWIG\_IsOK(res)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{      // success code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{    \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{      // fail code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{   which is the same really, but now you can also do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{    Type *ptr;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{    int res = SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj,(void **)(\&ptr),ty.flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{    if (SWIG\_IsOK(res)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{      // success code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{      if (SWIG\_IsNewObj(res) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{        ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{    delete *ptr;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{      \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{        ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{      \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00228}00228 \textcolor{comment}{    \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00229}00229 \textcolor{comment}{      // fail code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00230}00230 \textcolor{comment}{    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00231}00231 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00232}00232 \textcolor{comment}{   I.e., now SWIG\_ConvertPtr can return new objects and you can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00233}00233 \textcolor{comment}{   identify the case and take care of the deallocation. Of course that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00234}00234 \textcolor{comment}{   also requires SWIG\_ConvertPtr to return new result values, such as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00235}00235 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00236}00236 \textcolor{comment}{      int SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj, ptr,...) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00237}00237 \textcolor{comment}{        if (<obj is ok>) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00238}00238 \textcolor{comment}{          if (<need new object>) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00239}00239 \textcolor{comment}{            *ptr = <ptr to new allocated object>;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00240}00240 \textcolor{comment}{            return SWIG\_NEWOBJ;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00241}00241 \textcolor{comment}{          \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00242}00242 \textcolor{comment}{            *ptr = <ptr to old object>;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00243}00243 \textcolor{comment}{            return SWIG\_OLDOBJ;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00244}00244 \textcolor{comment}{          \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{        \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{          return SWIG\_BADOBJ;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00247}00247 \textcolor{comment}{        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{comment}{      \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00249}00249 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{   Of course, returning the plain '0(success)/-\/1(fail)' still works, but you can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{comment}{   more explicit by returning SWIG\_BADOBJ, SWIG\_ERROR or any of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00252}00252 \textcolor{comment}{   SWIG errors code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00253}00253 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{   Finally, if the SWIG\_CASTRANK\_MODE is enabled, the result code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00255}00255 \textcolor{comment}{   allows returning the 'cast rank', for example, if you have this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00256}00256 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00257}00257 \textcolor{comment}{       int food(double)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00258}00258 \textcolor{comment}{       int fooi(int);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00259}00259 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00260}00260 \textcolor{comment}{   and you call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00261}00261 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00262}00262 \textcolor{comment}{      food(1)   // cast rank '1'  (1 -\/> 1.0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00263}00263 \textcolor{comment}{      fooi(1)   // cast rank '0'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00264}00264 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00265}00265 \textcolor{comment}{   just use the SWIG\_AddCast()/SWIG\_CheckState()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00266}00266 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00267}00267 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00268}\mbox{\hyperlink{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_af9ecbac56d4c5cd6104ae8f6bb82e9f7}{00268}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SWIG\_OK                    (0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00269}00269 \textcolor{comment}{/* Runtime errors are < 0 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00270}\mbox{\hyperlink{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_acfa11a770d66f9ca6ba170b173c56c94}{00270}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SWIG\_ERROR                 (-\/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00271}00271 \textcolor{comment}{/* Errors in range -\/1 to -\/99 are in swigerrors.swg (errors for all languages including those not using the runtime) */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00272}00272 \textcolor{comment}{/* Errors in range -\/100 to -\/199 are language specific errors defined in *errors.swg */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00273}00273 \textcolor{comment}{/* Errors < -\/200 are generic runtime specific errors */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00299}00299 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(SWIG\_CASTRANK\_MODE)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00536}00536 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00537}00537 \textcolor{comment}{  Search for a swig\_type\_info structure only by mangled name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00538}00538 \textcolor{comment}{  Search is a O(log \#types)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l00539}00539 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02809}02809 \textcolor{comment}{/* -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ TYPE CONVERSION AND EQUIVALENCE RULES (END) -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02810}02810 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02811}02811 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02812}02812 \textcolor{comment}{/* -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02813}02813 \textcolor{comment}{ * Type initialization:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02814}02814 \textcolor{comment}{ * This problem is tough by the requirement that no dynamic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02815}02815 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory is used. Also, since swig\_type\_info structures store pointers to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02816}02816 \textcolor{comment}{ * swig\_cast\_info structures and swig\_cast\_info structures store pointers back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02817}02817 \textcolor{comment}{ * to swig\_type\_info structures, we need some lookup code at initialization.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02818}02818 \textcolor{comment}{ * The idea is that swig generates all the structures that are needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02819}02819 \textcolor{comment}{ * The runtime then collects these partially filled structures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02820}02820 \textcolor{comment}{ * The SWIG\_InitializeModule function takes these initial arrays out of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02821}02821 \textcolor{comment}{ * swig\_module, and does all the lookup, filling in the swig\_module.types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02822}02822 \textcolor{comment}{ * array with the correct data and linking the correct swig\_cast\_info}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02823}02823 \textcolor{comment}{ * structures together.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02824}02824 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02825}02825 \textcolor{comment}{ * The generated swig\_type\_info structures are assigned statically to an initial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02826}02826 \textcolor{comment}{ * array. We just loop through that array, and handle each type individually.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02827}02827 \textcolor{comment}{ * First we lookup if this type has been already loaded, and if so, use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02828}02828 \textcolor{comment}{ * loaded structure instead of the generated one. Then we have to fill in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02829}02829 \textcolor{comment}{ * cast linked list. The cast data is initially stored in something like a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02830}02830 \textcolor{comment}{ * two-\/dimensional array. Each row corresponds to a type (there are the same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02831}02831 \textcolor{comment}{ * number of rows as there are in the swig\_type\_initial array). Each entry in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02832}02832 \textcolor{comment}{ * a column is one of the swig\_cast\_info structures for that type.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02833}02833 \textcolor{comment}{ * The cast\_initial array is actually an array of arrays, because each row has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02834}02834 \textcolor{comment}{ * a variable number of columns. So to actually build the cast linked list,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02835}02835 \textcolor{comment}{ * we find the array of casts associated with the type, and loop through it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02836}02836 \textcolor{comment}{ * adding the casts to the list. The one last trick we need to do is making}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02837}02837 \textcolor{comment}{ * sure the type pointer in the swig\_cast\_info struct is correct.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02838}02838 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02839}02839 \textcolor{comment}{ * First off, we lookup the cast-\/>type name to see if it is already loaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02840}02840 \textcolor{comment}{ * There are three cases to handle:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02841}02841 \textcolor{comment}{ *  1) If the cast-\/>type has already been loaded AND the type we are adding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02842}02842 \textcolor{comment}{ *     casting info to has not been loaded (it is in this module), THEN we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02843}02843 \textcolor{comment}{ *     replace the cast-\/>type pointer with the type pointer that has already}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02844}02844 \textcolor{comment}{ *     been loaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02845}02845 \textcolor{comment}{ *  2) If BOTH types (the one we are adding casting info to, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02846}02846 \textcolor{comment}{ *     cast-\/>type) are loaded, THEN the cast info has already been loaded by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02847}02847 \textcolor{comment}{ *     the previous module so we just ignore it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02848}02848 \textcolor{comment}{ *  3) Finally, if cast-\/>type has not already been loaded, then we add that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02849}02849 \textcolor{comment}{ *     swig\_cast\_info to the linked list (because the cast-\/>type) pointer will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02850}02850 \textcolor{comment}{ *     be correct.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02851}02851 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l02852}02852 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l03011}03011 \textcolor{comment}{/* This function will propagate the clientdata field of type to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l03012}03012 \textcolor{comment}{* any new swig\_type\_info structures that have been added into the list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8cpp_source_l03013}03013 \textcolor{comment}{* of equivalent types.  It is like calling}}
